[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. The fuzzer entry point [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`DomXfaParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m fed crafted [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mPDF/XFA data into Apache PDFBox’s XFA parser [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`PDXFAResource.getDocument` → [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`DocumentBuilder.parse`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. During XML entity resolution, the standard Java HTTP client [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`HttpURLConnection` [0m[35m/[0m[39m `Socket.connect`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m attempted to open a TCP connection to [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m`.  [0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Jazzer’s `ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrfSocket` detected this outbound [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconnection as untrusted and raised an SSRF alert.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important observations  [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The network request originates from XML parsing of an XFA form, implying [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexternal entity or URL references are being resolved without restriction.  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The stack trace highlights the flow through [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`com.sun.org.apache.xerces.internal.*` XML classes into `HttpURLConnection`.  [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  - The SSRF sanitizer uses `ServerSideRequestForgery.checkSsrf` at the socket [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlevel, demonstrating that arbitrary host/port resolution from untrusted input is [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeing caught.[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code areas for review  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **PDFBox XFA Parsing**  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `org.apache.pdfbox.pdmodel.interactive.form.PDXFAResource.getDocument`  [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Underlying XML parsing configuration in `DocumentBuilderImpl` [0m[35m/[0m[39m Xerces.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. **Network Connection Logic**  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Standard Java HTTP client instantiation [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`HttpClient.New`, [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`HttpURLConnection.connect`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Any custom entity resolver or URL handler that may allow external [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mreferences.  [0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **Fuzzer Harness**  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `com.example.DomXfaParserFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mserves as entry but is [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot the root cause[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - Ensure harness does not inadvertently allow uncontrolled network access [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbeyond intended test scope.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mReviewing these components will give a holistic understanding of how untrusted [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mXFA/XML inputs can drive outbound network connections and trigger SSRF conditions.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAn SSRF vulnerability was detected during fuzzing of the PDFBox XFA parser: [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted XML content triggered an HTTP connection via standard `DocumentBuilder`, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mleading to a `FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium` from Jazzer’s SSRF sanitizer. A proposed [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpatch replaced manual use of `DocumentBuilderFactory` with a call to [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mXMLUtil.parse[0m[1;39m([0m[33m...[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and updated imports accordingly. After applying the patch, the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproject failed to compile with a syntax error in `PDXFAResource.java` [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`class, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minterface, or enum expected` at line [0m[1;36m138[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, indicating a misplaced or mismatched [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbrace or other structural issue.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Initial Issue  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - A fuzzing run of `DomXfaParserFuzzer` invoked `[0m[1;35mPDXFAResource.getDocument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`.  [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - During XML parsing, the JDK’s `HttpURLConnection` was used implicitly [0m[1;39m([0m[39mvia [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mentity resolution[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, triggering Jazzer’s SSRF sanitizer.  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The sanitizer raised `FuzzerSecurityIssueMedium: Server Side Request Forgery [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mSSRF[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` when attempting to connect to `jazze.com:[0m[1;36m80[0m[39m`.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Stack trace highlights calls from `XMLParser.parse` back to [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`HttpURLConnection` and `Socket.connect`.[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Important Observations  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The vulnerability arises in XML entity resolution, not in the fuzz harness [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mitself.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The call site is `[0m[1;35mPDXFAResource.getDocument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, which builds and invokes a [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstandard DOM parser.  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - External entity resolution is not disabled, allowing network requests based on[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39muntrusted input.[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Attempt  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Imports updated: removed `ParserConfigurationException` import, added [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.pdfbox.util.XMLUtil`.  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Method `[0m[1;35mgetDocument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` refactored from manually creating a [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`DocumentBuilderFactory` and `DocumentBuilder` to a single call:  [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```java[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     public Document [0m[1;35mgetDocument[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException [0m[1;39m{[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         return [0m[1;35mXMLUtil.parse[0m[1;39m([0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             new [0m[1;35mByteArrayInputStream[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mthis.getBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m,[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m             true[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m         [0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Removed `try–catch` block handling `ParserConfigurationException` and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`SAXException`.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Patch Result and Log  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Compilation failed with:  [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     PDXFAResource.java:[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;36m138[0m[39m,[0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m][0m[39m class, interface, or enum expected[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```  [0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
